I used to live right next door to this place and loved it! They have a different menu during the week than their Saturday brunch but both menus are great.

Off their weekday menu, I've had a few of their breakfast burritos and they are so yummy. On the weekend menu I've had the quiche, the katsu, a sort of moco loco special, and a kimchi dish... all amazing, but my favorite was the French toast! Sooo good!

I really like the aesthetic of this place and the staff seem very friendly. I highly recommend this place for breakfast.<//Text>

< Review>
My quesadilla had big portions and good flavor. I also ordered a Mr Rosa Breakfast Burrito to go for my dad to go and he loved it. Customer service is also great because they asked me if I wanted the burrito to be cooked a little later so it could more fresh for later. I will be coming back to try more.

Been back since and have enjoyed the tuna melt. The bread for the tuna melt is toasted perfectly!

They have a rotating lunch special and this week (June 27, 2019) it was a rosemary porchetta sandwich. Soft buns, thinly sliced prochetta, great flavor.

July 25, 2019
Today I had their Mozart Burger. Again, you can really taste the top notch ingredients that David and his team use. The patty had a nice beefy flavor. The tomato was oven dried and seasoned. The fries were perfectly crisp.< /Review>

I came in and ordered a strawberry napoleon and a slice of german chocolate cake.

The napoleon was a bit light on the strawberries but was delicious nonetheless. They obviously used decent whipped cream and nothing stood out as being nasty.

The german chocolate cake, on the other hand, was the worst I've had in my lifetime.
In the semi-transparent coconut topping, there is VERY little coconut. most of it is a sugary goop. But there's a likely reason they kept the actual coconut flavor so minimal: they couldn't drown out the minimal amount of chocolate flavor. It tasted like one of those cake mixes that uses preservatives. I'd bet ten dollars that they bought that german chocolate cake from elsewhere and marked up the price significantly.
I could even taste the baking powder/soda residue, which competes with intensity with actual chocolate flavor. That cake was sugar, flour, and baking soda. Oh and some coconut and chocolate. Well how am I suppose to have a cake tasting with no cake?? So anyway I left & right down the street was Sunrise so we decided to go in and set up an appointment & maybe grab a slice of cake to go. This place was so amazing they literally set up a tasting in like 5 minutes!! They gave us 5 different cakes & about 10 different fillings. The hazelnut is DEEEELICIOUS! So we looked at some pictures & tweeked a little bit and came up with our perfect cake. The cost for a 3 tier w rhinestone toppers was about the same price as a 2 tier w no topper from Old Tyme & quite frankly tasted better ( I got a slice to go on the way out, which I paid for ) AND they reserved the date for my cake and said I could make payments in any increments as long as it was paid for 2 weeks before my date. Also, I was told by Old Tyme that they "couldn't make an ombre cake in buttercream, only fondant" but Sunrise said "no problem" so buttercream it is! Amazing customer service (Saragon took our cake order) and an amazing tasting product! Thank you Sunrise Bakery!! :)</text>

< Review>
Drinks and prices were as expected, but the wait time was terrible the day I visited.  I arrived and ordered right away, only one person was ahead of us and waiting, and there were 6 people working.  Shouldn't be too long right?

We stood there for more than half an hour as we saw 30+ drinks being made.  There was one order that had 7 of the same drink and another with 5 of the same drink.  Then those drinks just sat on the counter, waiting to be picked up.  We had just ordered two simple drinks while there was literally all those drinks just sitting on the counter.  We were there long enough to watch an entire episode of Avatar: The Last Airbender.  Given that it was busy, it was understandable that it took awhile, however I think they should prioritize the people that were standing in the shop waiting for a drink, rather than making drinks that were just going to sit on the counter.

To clarify, the low rating is primarily for a system that does not prioritize small orders for people that are standing in the shop waiting for drinks while the staff makes huge batch orders that are just sitting on the counter waiting for pick up.  Some of the drinks that were sitting on the counter were still waiting for pick up when we left.</Review>
